      function mapa_city()
   {
      var myLatlng = new google.maps.LatLng(50.0881989,14.4240075);
      var myOptions =
         {
            zoom: 13,
            center: myLatlng,
            zoomControl: false,
            mapTypeId: google.maps.MapTypeId.ROADMAP
         };
      var map = new google.maps.Map(document.getElementById('mapa_city'),myOptions);
   }
function mapa()
   {
      var myLatlng = new google.maps.LatLng(50.0881989,14.4240075);
      var myOptions =
         {
            zoom: 13,
            center: {lat: 50.0881989, lng: 14.4240075},
            mapTypeControl: false,
            zoomControl: true,
            scrollwheel: false,
            streetViewControl: false,
            mapTypeId: google.maps.MapTypeId.ROADMAP
         };
      var map = new google.maps.Map(document.getElementById('mapa'),myOptions);
      var infowindow = new google.maps.InfoWindow();
      var marker, i;
      var bounds = new google.maps.LatLngBounds();
      var center = map.getCenter();
      google.maps.event.trigger(map, "resize");
      map.setCenter(center);
      google.maps.event.addDomListener(window, "resize", function() {
         var center = map.getCenter();
         google.maps.event.trigger(map, "resize");
         map.setCenter(center);
      });
      for (i = 0; i < markers.length; i++)
         {
            var pos = new google.maps.LatLng(markers[i][3], markers[i][4]);
            bounds.extend(pos);
            marker = new google.maps.Marker(
               {
                  position: pos,
                  map: map,
                  title: markers[i][1],
                  icon: 'images/mapsmarker.png'
               });
            google.maps.event.addListener(marker, 'mouseover', (function(marker, i)
               {
                  return function()
                     {
                        var point = fromLatLngToPoint(marker.getPosition(), map);
                        height = $(window).height()/2;
                        width = $(window).width()/4;
                        $('#gmtool').load('api/mapsmenu/?id='+markers[i][0]).css({'left': point.x-width, 'top': point.y-400-20}).show();
                     }
               })(marker, i));
            google.maps.event.addListener(marker, 'mouseout', (function(marker, i)
               {
                  return function() { document.getElementById('gmtool').style.display= 'none';  document.getElementById('gmtool').innerHTML = '';  }
               })(marker, i));
            google.maps.event.addListener(marker, 'click', (function(marker, i)
               {
                  return function() { window.location.href = markers[i][2]; }
               })(marker, i));
         }
      //map.fitBounds(bounds);
   }
